<review>The LBVBC of Rancho Santa Margarita is easy to get to off of the 241 toll road. On-street parking is a huge bonus as most other OC tournament locations only have paid parking. Staff are nice and check in goes fast. Inside is very cramped. Many courts do not have benches for players to sit on. The ceiling is very low, and trusses cause continual interference with play. Nets leave huge gaps between courts and balls are continually entering adjacent courts. <rating>5</rating>< Review>
Great dining experience! Nice little restaurant/retail spot with a great patio. Let's start with the great selection of esoteric wines. I'm from arizona and a lot of the wines here don't make it to our state, so this was a treasure trove of fun wine.

Service was great! Server was experienced and knowledgeable. Despite being new to Les Marchands he was up to date on the wine and food, obviously drawing from a well of experience. Beverage director was a wizard, well equipped to answer any and all questions and make sound suggestions.

Food was great. Ordered a Bottle of Tempier Bandol ros√©. Went great with a small veggie plate and charcuterie board. Everything was great! Server recommended the hand made spaghetti in a local uni butter sauce. So great! Simple and elegant, like pasta in Italy. Simple ingredient driven dish that was just fantastic. We were the first to order it and chief came out to ask what we thought. Just an example of the level of love and care that goes into the food here. Finished with the lamb meatballs and roasted tomatoes. Another simple and perfectly executed dish.

Forgot to mention, we showed up with two little people. Our two year old was running on fumes and started to lose his mind about half way through dinner. They didn't blink and handled it like pros.

Hats off to chef and the staff for a great dining experience! That pasta though....< /Review>

Its an amazing little store that has everything you need. It has every kind of materials from a variety of producers, from high quality fancy materials to cheap ones for the starving artists. < Text>
I've been coming here for over 20 years.  The Professional Discount they offer, really helps out a great deal when you're a struggling artist, and your supply's are pricey no matter what.
Nicky, the manager, and her entire team, are quite knowledgeable about the products they have, and if there's something you're looking for, but haven't found elsewhere.....ask if they'll order it.
Seriously, I've out orders in for French Curves they don't carry in regular stock, and within a week, they'd arrived at the store.  All Pre-Covid of course, but I doubt that that'd hinder you much from ordering anything.
And yes, their Prices are quite fair.  Cheaper than others in some instances, but I'll let you discover that for yourself.
Just tell Nickie that Billy Crooks sent 'ya.  It won't get you any more discounts.<//Text>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
This place is great.  Stopped in today looking for some brushes for my hobbying and the staff w super helpful.  Felt safe going in as they keep the customers limited to six at a time and are good about maintaining the rule.  The brush I was looking for was out of stock but one of the employees showed me several alternatives and even gave me a display bush to try out.

The only downside to this store is that it's a little more expensive than Blicks or Michaels but that small price is worth the kind of service you receive.  In this difficult time or I hope we all come out to support local small businesses like this one.< /text>

< text>
I was out for a road trip and found this place on accident. Pleasently surprised to find this place back in the Canyon. Beautiful location with a stream running under the Bar. We only had drinks, so I can't comment on food. Service was friendly. Locals were mostly keeping to themselves, but no one made me feel unwelcomed (which I have experienced at similar locations). This is a perfect spot to visit if you are out for a day ride. Also, drove through campground (adjacent to Bar) to check it out for future use. Camp host was super friendly. Definitely will come back to eat and camp.</text>

<userid>114507383135742253456< /userid>< name>
Stu Warford</name>
< Date>
1565758757900< /Date>
<Rate>5<//Rate><Text>Did a day road trip from Thousand Oaks to this place a few days ago.  Beautiful drive up through the mountains.  Although we're in August, the hills are still green and lovely.  Passed deer on the way up.  Got to Camp Scheideck Lodge right at lunch time on a week day.  Wasn't at all sure what to expect, although reviews were positive.  It's right between a set of small houses and a campground.  A small stream runs through the area.

The "lodge" is really a restaurant from what we can tell.  When we got there, there was one customer and one bar waiter.  The lodge has a lot of character and we were ready for lunch.

We (my wife and I) each ordered hamburgers, mine with fries and hers with a salad.  The servings were well presented and plentiful.  Not only did they look good, but they tasted excellent.  We were pleasantly surprised.

While we were eating, a couple of "regulars" came in and ordered as well.  The staff were very friendly with the regulars and with us as well.  While eating we asked several questions about the area, the campground, and a nearby trail.   The staff really were hospitable and showed interest in us and our questions.

By the time we left, we were well satisfied and felt really welcomed.  This proved to be a gem, and we've added it to our list of places to return to.<//Text><pics>None< /pics>< Response>
None< /Response>

<text>We just came here with a LivingSocial deal, and I completely have no idea how many stars I should give this place, because I feel like I'm writing 3 completely different reviews:

* The ping-pong: a lot of fun. Doesn't really feel like it would be worth 30 dollars an hour, but definitely feels like it would be worth the discounted rate that I checked, and it's still active as of last night if you check in on yelp. Playing ping-pong in a semi-club-like atmosphere, except more subdued (they don't play annoying techno music, and it's not so loud you can't hear your friends), is a lot of fun, especially since you also don't have to pick up your own balls if you don't feel like it. 5 stars (or at least would be with the yelp discount).

* The drinks: killer. We got two drinks with our deal. We got the two that came with the deal: one with a vodka, sweet bubbly wine and lychee; the other a truly remarkable gin-based drink with ginger, eggwhite, and added herbs - probably my favorite gin-based drink ever. After trying those, I had to order a third, as I had high hopes for a drink made with black pepper that had "peppery" in its name. Sadly, that one was a little disappointing: it was still a great drink, but I didn't really taste the pepper at all, just the other ingredients (lemon, cucumber and sugar). Still, 5 stars for drinks, despite being a little pricey (12 dollars as of last night). Drinks were served pretty much immediately, with a smile, and were pretty potent.

* The food: highly disappointing. The deal also came with two appetizers, and for what we got, we would have been about as happy just paying the yelp price for the table, and regular price for drinks. We tried the ahi skewers and the mini chicken bahn mi, and while neither were actually *bad*, both were pretty lackluster, and *tiny*. 4 tiny ahi skewers that were kinda tasteless and looked like they'd been preserved somehow (though admittedly their wasabi/avacado dip was quite good), and 6 slider sandwiches, by which I mean actually on slider-type bread as well as being bite-sized, that didn't really taste like they had much in the way of bahn mi stuff in them, they basically just tasted like chicken sliders (other than one, and not the other five, had a sliver of rather potent jalapeno in it, which was a great surprise.) There is no way I would ever consider paying 12 dollars for these! 2 stars for food (because they weren't actually gross, just disappointing.)

So basically, this is a fun place to go, play some ping-pong, get some fancy mixed drinks, and *not* order any food.</text>< Pics>

<Review>I had never tried Afghan food before eating here. I'm a big fan of Mediterranean / Persian / Turkish food, so I figured I would try it. I am certainly glad I did.

The food was great - I had the fried potatoes as an appetizer, and I had the beef meatballs as a main course. Both were subtle and delicious - the kind of food that begs you to have just one more bite. The rice is perfectly cooked, and when mixed with the sauce it makes a wonderful combination.

For dessert I had the baklava and a cup of cardamom tea. Both were a perfect endnote to a great meal.

The service was also perfect - attentive yet allowed for privacy. The owner was very welcoming and very helpful.

Also, the prices are really good, especially for the area. I can't recommend this place enough!</Review><Pics>None</Pics>< resp>

<rate>5< /rate><gmapID>0x80dbf917070bede7:0x4b94cd98bd9e604f</gmapID><text>Absolutely delicious! Everything we had was just terrific. I can't believe the place was so empty while we were there for dinner. If you have not tried this place yet, you are really missing out on some good food. We had two of the appetizers - Sambosa (ground beef, chickpeas & herbs) and Bolani - very yummy. Be sure to try these with the spicy chutney-like sauce. The sauce is only a little spicy but oh-so good, even on your main dish. Then we had the lamb with eggplant (Badenjan Chalow). The lamb was so tender, it flaked from the bone easily with a fork and was really flavorful. The eggplant was superb - I only wish more came with the dish. We also had a Meatball dish (Kafta Chalow), which was also incredibly good. The rice served with each dish was cooked perfectly and was an ample amount. Even the black tea we had was really good. It was a perfect accompaniment to the meal. Service was great too! I highly recommend this place!</text></record></dataset><record>

Nurses were awesome post Microdisectomy for my back. They took good care of me, made sure I got what I needed and took the time to get to know me. For the most part the nurses took the time to build a relationship (shout out to Kayla and Allison) for being pretty new but going above and beyond.

Service was crazy fast. Got mri, X-ray, blood work done within a few hours. That would have taken days outside of the ER. Got into a room pretty fast as well. All nurses and techs very professional.

I gave a 3 because of the COVID protocols. I was able to walk out of the room several times without a mask and when I was literally being wheeled into the operating table they found out I didn‚Äôt get a COVID test. I had to wait two hours in OP prep until my rapid results came in. Extremely disappointed the hospital missed that. Sitting in pre op with more time to think about what can go wrong wasn‚Äôt cool. I believe this was a miss by ER dr not the surgery team.

I would however attend the hospital again if I needed another visit.</review>
